Accessibility digest

Synopsis
PageMaplewood Senior Living contact form
URLhttps://www.maplewoodseniorliving.com/contact/
Requesterpool@jpdev.pro
Test date2023/04/23
Score863
Tested byTestaro, procedure ts24
Scored byTestilo, procedure tsp24
Digested byTestilo, procedure tdp24

Introduction

This is a digest of results from a battery of accessibility Tests.

The battery includes 1353 automated accessibility tests drawn from ten different packages: Alfa, Axe, Continuum, Equal Access, HTML CodeSniffer, Nu Html Checker, QualWeb, Tenon, Testaro, and WAVE.

These tests were run on the web page named above and gave the page a score of 863, where 0 would be perfect.

Issue summary

Special issues

log: Score 41. This is based on the amount of browser error logging and miscellaneous logging during the tests.

preventions: Score 100. This is based on tests that the page did not allow to be run. That impedes accessibility progress and risks interfering with tools that users with disabilities need.

Classified issues

Issue focusIndication

WCAG: 2.4.7

Score: 165

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test focInd, score 127 (Focused element displays no or a nostandard focus indicator)
  • Package alfa, test r65, score 44 (Element in the sequential focus order has no visible focus)
  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R62, score 45 (Element in the sequential focus order has no visible focus)

Issue contentBeyondLandmarks

WCAG: 1.3.6

Score: 50

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package axe, test region, score 30 (Some page content is not contained by landmarks)
  • Package ibm, test Rpt_Aria_OrphanedContent_Native_Host_Sematics, score 36 (Content does not reside within an element with a landmark role)

Issue fontSizeAbsolute

WCAG: 1.4.4

Score: 34

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r74, score 32 (Paragraph text has an absolute font size)

Issue linkIndication

WCAG: 1.3.3

Score: 31

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test linkUl, score 29 (Non-underlined adjacent links)

Issue linkNoText

WCAG: 2.4.4

Score: 29

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.4_1_2.H91.A.NoContent, score 8 (Link has an href attribute but no text)
  • Package ibm, test WCAG20_A_HasText, score 4 (Hyperlink has no text description)
  • Package wave, test e:link_empty, score 16 (Link contains no text)
  • Package tenon, test 57, score 16 (Link has no text inside it)

Issue targetSize

WCAG: 2.5.5

Score: 29

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package tenon, test 152, score 27 (Actionable element is smaller than the minimum required size)

Issue titleBad

WCAG: 1.3.1

Score: 26

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test titledEl, score 24 (title attribute belongs to an inappropriate element)

Issue inputOnlyPlaceholder

WCAG: 4.1.2

Score: 26

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package continuum, test 863, score 24 (input has an accessible name that depends on a placeholder)

WCAG: 1.4.4

Score: 26

Issue reports in this category:

Score: 22

Score: 15

Issue repeatedContentRisk

WCAG: 2.4.1

Score: 11

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r87, score 1 (First focusable element is not a link to the main content)
  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R73, score 1 (Block of repeated content is not collapsible)
  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R74, score 1 (Document has no instrument to move focus to non-repeated content)
  • Package qualWeb, test QW-BP17, score 7 (No link at the beginning of a block of repeated content goes to the end of the block)
